  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f26593ec-c29e-41af-ad47-0774b411abf1'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1712687984" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16006558144939605483">3.5 stars...rounding up.<br/><br/>I could have read a whole book about the first semester. That was good stuff. I understand you have to get from point A to B, but once it got past the wedding, that plotline really started to move. Personally I enjoyed the story more than the sex, not saying the sex scenes were bad...just the story(for me) was better. Kinda the same way as Dom Wars. <br/></span>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1145078944" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1145078944" />
    <a title="Mackenzie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12601799-mackenzie"><img alt="Mackenzie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586575570p2/12601799.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1145078944?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mackenzie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mackenzie" href="/user/show/12601799-mackenzie">Mackenzie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1145078944" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5873463053621914582">I've never been so engaged with some books. But LET MEH TELL YOU! <br/>Lucian W Bane's White Knight Dom Academy (continuation of Dom Wars), continues the story of Tara and Lucian with some southern twang to it and best of all GRAMS! Also Steve is out back into the mix and he comes with the best conversations when talking to Lucian. Let's just talk about the elephant in the room, shall we? <span id="freeTextContainer1788064245078175505"><div>

    <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419981633i/13152280.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  </a>
</div><br/><br/>I have stopped setting expectations when it comes to the books Lucian writes, each time he not only exceeds them but blows them out of the water! <br/><br/>White Knight Dom Academy is a continuation of the ever popular Dom Wars series and brings back our favorite characters Lucian, Tara & Steve as well as introducing us to a spitfire Gramma and Steve's wife Susan. WKA picks up just a few weeks after where DW left off and it can be read starting with WKA but I would suggest you reading the DW s</span>
  <span id="freeText1788064245078175505" style="display:none"><div>
  <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-buhzxmCrYx0/VKMy_QINc2I/AAAAAAAACIM/aFSThPVnAnQ/s1600/wka%2Breview.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419981633i/13152280.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div><br><br>I have stopped setting expectations when it comes to the books Lucian writes, each time he not only exceeds them but blows them out of the water! <br><br>White Knight Dom Academy is a continuation of the ever popular Dom Wars series and brings back our favorite characters Lucian, Tara &amp; Steve as well as introducing us to a spitfire Gramma and Steve's wife Susan. WKA picks up just a few weeks after where DW left off and it can be read starting with WKA but I would suggest you reading the DW series first or else a lot of stuff won't make sense to you. <br><br>Lucian &amp; Tara are finally out of the competition and are now millionaires but there is a few little stipulations they didn't know about in order to receive all of their money. Never ones to back down from a challenge they decide to figure out a way to do this and of course that means bringing in their trusty sidekick Steve. With plans on running Gramma's farm and the wedding coming up they have the perfect way to bring Steve in before telling him he is going to be hanging out with Betty again. <br><br>In this continuation Lucian &amp; Tara are coming more into themselves and who they are in the relationship. There isn't a huge focus on roles and Tara is still getting over some of her own insecurities. They are adorable, and mushy, and sickening at times but they are so so hot! I think the sex scenes in this one are electrifying at times, you can see that they are in love, full of passion and trust each other 100%. It changes the dynamics of sex, they are not simply fucking one another they are owning and worshiping each other. <br><br>This book is romantic, entertaining and hilarious! There were more than a few times that I was laughing aloud. Lucian has this amazing talent of bringing his characters to life and writing some of the best characters that I have ever read. Ones that will stick with you for a long time and make you sad to see their story end. Do yourself a favor and read this book, it will be a hot &amp; hilarious 3 hours!! <br><br>Relentlessbookchic approved &amp; recommended.<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/relentlessbookchic">http://www.facebook.com/relentlessboo...</a></span>

  <span id="freeText528599103254013411" style="display:none">5 stars<br />☆☆☆☆☆<br /><br />Tara &amp; Lucian's story continues after their win and become Gladiator's Top Dom &amp; Domme. After meeting with the head of Gladiator they are now dealing with consequences of not reading the asterisked area on the Dom Wars contract. Headed home to collect Gramma from the nursing home they also have to figure out how they are going to successfully pull off their new tasks. With the risk of failing and losing their money they know exactly who they need to pull this job off, Steve!<br />WKDA does not disappoint. You will absolutely love White Knight Dom Academy. The whittiness is amped up and you will giggle at every turn.   <span id="freeText11986547285268202631" style="display:none">Author Lucian Bane puts his own stamp on a truly erotic, romantic twist on a tale of two soul mates continuing to build their everlasting relationship on a foundation of trust and communication as they fight to spread awareness to couples and families on the healing power of love. Together with a little help from family and friends they will strive to teach couples how to fight the good fight on the ways to connect; physically, mentally, and spiritually. <br /><br />The Author really puts his own unique style in bringing this loving couple to life. Lucian and Tara are finally getting married, growing their family bond, conquering their family “Farm” and sustaining their quirking friendships all while earning the “Winnings” from Gladiator Inc. You can really feel the emotion with every word you read, you feel the smoldering heat the couple shows each other, and laugh your ass off at the hilarious banter each character brings!<br /><br />Thank You Lucian Bane, you truly brought me Love, Peace, and Joy!</span>

To find the screenshots, simply search for "Lucian W Bane".<br /><br /><br />Review from the author's Facebook page before it was deleted:<br /><br /><br />"Social media can make or break you. And it looks like you are insistent that you don't care about your reputation as a human being or a professional author. Attacking your fans for not buying your work, threatening to kick them out for not promoting you, sending harrassing messages to fans and calling them bitches is beyond disgraceful. I'm not a fan of your attitude and I most certainly am not going to support you or waste a single penny on your work. There's no need to "purge" me. I'm already long gone.<br /><br /><br />Also, the author appears to have removed the offensive post. Check the other recommendations for screenshots. In the future, think before you post. The internet never forgets."</span>

Lucian and Tara go home to get Grannie and make their lives together but what follows is funny, Hot and oh so beautiful! This is a book you will not be able to put down and will long for the second book. Lucian knows what is important and puts his heart into his stories.</span>

  <span id="freeText7775123479855181150" style="display:none">White Knight Dom Academy is the first book in the spin off from Dom Wars. Now we get to see Tara and Lucian out in the real world; however they have learnt there are conditions to gain their prize money from Gladiator Inc. Lucian and Tara have to train up 5 couples in the D/s lifestyle over the next 5 years and sell a lot of products to Tara's home town, a southern town in the bible belt!<br /><br />It's great to have Tara and Lucian together outside of Dom Wars, figuring out their relationship outside of the competition, their sex is hotter than ever, wow!. Lucian as always is completely devoted to Tara and persistently proving to her she is the only woman for him. Finally Tara can bring her Gramma home and she is a woman full of Sass and watching her interact with Luscious (her name for Lucian) is entertaining for sure. We get to see Lucian and Tara forge their way through the pivitol steps in their relationship to be bound to each other for life and love whilst being faced with the challenge of setting up their Dom academy.<br /></span>

  <span id="freeText17805122948671527079" style="display:none"><strong>Lucian &amp;Tara continues in White Dom Academy 1st Semester</strong><br /><br />After reading all 6 Dom Wars which is like a 'Survivor'-type competition, the winners Lucian Bane and Tara Reese find out they are required to fulfill the fine print. Train 5 couples in 5 years the art of D/s as well as well sell their insane ridiculous sex toys. Other difficult obstacles include: these classes must take place in Tara's hypocritical, pious, uptight, upstanding religious town; classes must be recorded; must have all items from catalog sold complete with delivery confirmation and verification of sales. <br /><br />The story segues from winning the competition to the first semester.               >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5187322850014193781"><strong>Absolutly mind blowing</strong><br/><br/>I will say this omg... I have never felt such a connection with a story before. This book is phenomenal, I could not put it down. The love that poor's from each page was magical. The lust filled scenes will leave you breathless. Panties not required any where near this book. Lucian Bane is a true teacher and has earned the title the WHITE KNIGHT.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('JCqsKZbJvPOpbOE62ZauT+sZbRRuacqxNoYAVQS6cRnL95nu3wz3igWazrjPIVjpjGkz2BN/nvnAVWgoD8dDqA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
